package com.wildplot.android.rendering;

import com.wildplot.android.rendering.graphics.wrapper.FontMetricsWrap;
import com.wildplot.android.rendering.graphics.wrapper.GraphicsWrap;
import com.wildplot.android.rendering.graphics.wrapper.RectangleWrap;
import com.wildplot.android.rendering.interfaces.Drawable;
import java.text.DecimalFormat;
import br.ufmg.labsoft.mutvariants.listeners.ListenerUtil;

/**
 * This Class represents a Drawable x-axis
 */
public class XAxis implements Drawable {

    private boolean isIntegerNumbering = false;

    /**
     * believe it or not, this axis can be placed higher or lower than y=0
     */
    private double yOffset = 0;

    /**
     * Name of axis
     */
    private String name = "X";

    private boolean mHasName = false;

    /**
     * Format that is used to print numbers under markers
     */
    private final DecimalFormat df = new DecimalFormat("##0.0#");

    /**
     * format for very big or small values
     */
    private final DecimalFormat dfScience = new DecimalFormat("0.0##E0");

    private final DecimalFormat dfInteger = new DecimalFormat("#.#");

    /**
     * is set to true if scientifiv format (e.g. 1E-3) should be used
     */
    private boolean isScientific = false;

    /**
     * the PlotSheet object the x-axis is drawn onto
     */
    private final PlotSheet plotSheet;

    /**
     * the start of x-axis marker, used for relative alignment of further marks
     */
    private final double ticStart;

    /**
     * the space between two marks
     */
    private final double tic;

    /**
     * the space between two minor marks
     */
    private final double minorTic;

    /**
     * the estimated size between two major tics in auto tic mode
     */
    private float pixelDistance = 25;

    /**
     * start of drawn x-axis
     */
    private double start = 0;

    /**
     * end of drawn x-axis
     */
    private double end = 100;

    /**
     * true if the marker should be drawn into the direction above the axis
     */
    private final boolean markOnUpside = true;

    /**
     * true if the marker should be drawn into the direction under the axis
     */
    private boolean markOnDownside = true;

    /**
     * length of a marker in pixel, length is only for one side
     */
    private final float markerLength = 5;

    /**
     * true if this  axis is drawn onto the frame
     */
    private boolean isOnFrame = false;

    private String[] mTickNameList = null;

    private double[] mTickPositions = null;

    /**
     * Constructor for an X-axis object
     *
     * @param plotSheet the sheet the axis will be drawn onto
     * @param ticStart  the start of the axis markers used for relative alignment of other markers
     * @param tic       the space between two markers
     */
    public XAxis(PlotSheet plotSheet, double ticStart, double tic, double minorTic) {
        this.plotSheet = plotSheet;
        this.ticStart = ticStart;
        this.tic = tic;
        this.minorTic = minorTic;
    }

    public void paint(GraphicsWrap g) {
        RectangleWrap field = g.getClipBounds();
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27540)) {
            start = plotSheet.getxRange()[0];
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27541)) {
            end = plotSheet.getxRange()[1];
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27543)) {
            if (this.isOnFrame) {
                if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27542)) {
                    yOffset = plotSheet.getyRange()[0];
                }
            }
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27548)) {
            this.pixelDistance = Math.abs((ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27547) ? (plotSheet.xToGraphic(0, field) % plotSheet.xToGraphic(tic, field)) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27546) ? (plotSheet.xToGraphic(0, field) / plotSheet.xToGraphic(tic, field)) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27545) ? (plotSheet.xToGraphic(0, field) * plotSheet.xToGraphic(tic, field)) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27544) ? (plotSheet.xToGraphic(0, field) + plotSheet.xToGraphic(tic, field)) : (plotSheet.xToGraphic(0, field) - plotSheet.xToGraphic(tic, field)))))));
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27561)) {
            if ((ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27559) ? ((ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27553) ? (this.tic >= 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27552) ? (this.tic <= 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27551) ? (this.tic > 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27550) ? (this.tic != 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27549) ? (this.tic == 1e-2) : (this.tic < 1e-2)))))) && (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27558) ? (this.tic >= 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27557) ? (this.tic <= 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27556) ? (this.tic < 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27555) ? (this.tic != 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27554) ? (this.tic == 1e2) : (this.tic > 1e2))))))) : ((ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27553) ? (this.tic >= 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27552) ? (this.tic <= 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27551) ? (this.tic > 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27550) ? (this.tic != 1e-2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27549) ? (this.tic == 1e-2) : (this.tic < 1e-2)))))) || (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27558) ? (this.tic >= 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27557) ? (this.tic <= 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27556) ? (this.tic < 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27555) ? (this.tic != 1e2) : (ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27554) ? (this.tic == 1e2) : (this.tic > 1e2))))))))) {
                if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27560)) {
                    this.isScientific = true;
                }
            }
        }
        float[] coordStart = plotSheet.toGraphicPoint(start, yOffset, field);
        float[] coordEnd = plotSheet.toGraphicPoint(end, yOffset, field);
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27563)) {
            if (!this.isOnFrame) {
                if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27562)) {
                    g.drawLine(coordStart[0], coordStart[1], coordEnd[0], coordEnd[1]);
                }
            }
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27564)) {
            drawMarkers(g);
        }
        if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27566)) {
            if (mTickPositions == null) {
                if (!ListenerUtil.mutListener.listen(27565)) {
                    drawMinorMarkers(g);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /**

        }
    }

    }
